 The problem is that a large part of this information is rubbish, some of it is fatal to both individuals and society, and in this sea of rubbish, the platforms we rely on to reach the islands of information are being used by people everywhere
 Struggling to save from abuse, and sometimes it seems that they are not only supporting problematic material and behavior, but also expanding it
 i am
 aisi sthiti karodon bharatiyon ko soochna tak pahunch ke maamle main to behatar he lekin isi ke saath yah unhen har tarah ke nae khataron ke aage laachaar bana detii he
 These threats are sometimes well-known and outdated, such as greedy to gain, political powers or people with some narrow mindset, who remain active for the sake of the satisfaction they get from attempting to assert their perceived superiority over others, or else such threats Are those businesses operating in the way of digital media technology or behind the platform of related platforms, or the tools and systems Emal mounting manner
 kya samasyaayein hai?online uplabdh bahut sari jaankariyon ke liye 'bakawaas' to kuch acha shabd he, lekin, koi agar hamaare daur ke muddon ko thik-thik samajhnaa chaahe to isamen uske bahut saare fark chup jate hai
 a clearer definition has been brought by Claire Wardley and Hussein Darshan, which are 'fake information' (false but not intentionally inserted), 'misinformation' (intentionally spreading false information) and 'misinformation' (information that is complete Or may be partially true but is intended to harm someone)
 in vibhinn prakaaron kii samasyamoolak saamagree ko alag-alag halkon se vividh uddeshyon se taiyaar or prachaarit kiya jaataa he
 For the benefit of fake information, propaganda and misinformation, it is sometimes broadcasted by new circles and sometimes by the established media, which is very sad
 ('farji khabaren' kya hoti hai? yah poochne par bahut-se log ghatiya patrakarita yaa bhrasht yaa laalach se prerit sampadakeey taur-tareekon kii ore sanket karenge
 ) All these categories of information are used by political leaders and their supporters to gain power

 ) Finally, the most complicated thing is that people themselves sometimes pursue fake information, propaganda and misinformation as correct
 (is baat kaa koi vaigyanik pramaan nahin he ki kisi bhi tarah kaa mutr, maanav yaa anya stanpayi jaanwaron kaa, cancer kaa ilaaj kar saktaa he, lekin kuch log aisa daawa prachaarit karnaa jari rakhte hai, or amuman puure vishwaas tathaa gambhirtha ke saath
 ) Apart from all this, there are other problems which are not related to the truth of the information, but to the style of emphasizing the dark side of its interpretation
 masalan, jab hamamen se kuch log, kabhi bahut sakriy hokar, kabhi bade paimaane par or kabhi ek saath jutakar kisi ko uski nasl, dharm, ling, jati vagairah ko lekar nishaanaa banaate hai
 Its most ugly face is seen in hate speeches and literature, which incite violence, which sometimes results in bloody conflicts
 puraani samasyaayein, nai samasyaayenye sabhi puraani samasyaayein hai
 Sometimes some publishers mislead people, sometimes some powerful leaders lie and propagate it, sometimes some of us willfully or unknowingly pursue false and misleading things
 or, hamaara aapasi talmail aksar nahin hota, or kabhi-kabhi ham sakriy rup se ek-duusare ko nicha dikhaane, apamaanit karne yaa sharminda karne kii koshish karte hai
 But there are also new things that have to do with how and through the paths of online rubbish in search of islands of information relevant to us
 haal hi main maine apane sahyogiyon ke saath bharat main angreji bhashaa ke internet upyogkartaaon kaa jo surveykshan kiya, vah is mudde kii vyakhya behatar tareeke se kar saktaa he
 In the pre-digital era, we usually turned directly to newspaper-magazines and radio-tv for information on public affairs
 lekin online daur main aisa nahin he
 Only 18 percent of the Indian people in our survey said that they go directly to newspaper-magazines or radio-tv websites or apps as the main way of searching online news
 iske vipareet, 32 fisad kaa kahana tha ki ve search injanon par bharosa karte hai tathaa 24 fisad logon ne soshal media par bharosa jataayaa tha
 This means that companies like Google and Facebook are today more important online gatekeepers than any editor in India in terms of information and news
 yah sthiti purv-digital duniya se bahut alag he
 This research documents how both search engines and social media generally lead people to other news than they seek, and it is also documented that people do not always know that they have news Who are the givers, due to which they become the victims of propaganda, when they click on anything, identify its source or know its credibility and intentions behind it
 They are affected by it only
 nai samasyaayein yaheen nahin samaapt hotin
 The increase in the number of companies providing digital media and platforms has not only changed our ways of receiving information, but has also changed the way we connect or use them
 bharatiyon ne soshal media tathaa miseging plateform main paraspar samvaad karne tathaa usamen sakriy bhagidaari karne kii lalak dikhaai he or hamaare surveykshan main badi sankhya main logon ne suchit kiya ki ve fasebuk tathaa whatsap jaise plateformon par samachar saajha karte hai or mitron tathaa aparichiton se samakaleen muddon par charchaa ke liye unka upyog karte hai
 All this happens mostly without any maliciousness (or in some cases without any thought or consideration)
 yah badi baat he ki log keval suchanaaen hasil hi nahin kar sakate balki un par dusron ke saath charchaa bhi kar sakate hai

 isse vishesh rup se bante hue samaajon or dhruvikaran vaale rajnatik maahaul main badi baari samasya paidaa hoti he
 Indian people have no idea how compelled they are in this new and changing media environment
 hamaare surveykshan main se aadhe yaa usase bhi adhik logon ne kaha ki ve rajnatik dushprachaar, farji khabaron tathaa juthi or bhraamak samaacharon vaali ghatiya online patrakarita se chintit hai
 This apprehension and doubt will be justified in view of the many incidents of refugee media and 'paid news' in the face of political pressure
 isse bhi chintaa kii baat yah he ki bahut-se log dare hue hai

 So, what is the solution? What can we do in such a situation? In this ocean of information availability and abundance of nonsense, it is not easy to find islands of right information
 iske alaava samasya yah bhi he ki internet par uchit jagahon tak pahunchane ke liye ham jin plateformon par bharosa karte hai, ve companiyaan hi kai baar logon ko nishaanaa banane or dushprachaar ko badhaava dene lagati hai
 In such a situation, how can the Internet be made the most out of all this? Some of these challenges have been very old and always present, especially in diverse cultural and divided societies, which are often inseparable parts of our lives, in which we are often right and wrong
 Do not agree with each other and where important information for one person can be considered nonsense or dangerous by another person
 in muddon par ham shaayad kabhi ekarey nahin honge

 'tehran has told Islamabad that Iran will not be part of any such military alliance
